However, please note that the passenger in whose name the ticket is booked should carry a proof of his identity (along with the ticket) at the time of boarding the bus.</p> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> What are the different payment options available on Bus Ticket booking? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <ul><li>There are many payment modes available to book buses on the redBus website and app. Some of these payment modes that are available for the bus ticket booking process are:Debit Card/Credit Card/ATM Cards (Visa, MasterCard, Maestro &amp; Rupay)</li><li>Net Banking (HDFC Bank, ICICI Bank, Indian Bank, Axis Bank, SBI and all major banks)</li><li>UPI (Google Pay, Amazon Pay, PhonePe)&nbsp;</li><li>Book Now, Pay Later (Simpl)</li><li>Wallets (Paytm)Make sure to check the coupon code to get the discounts on bus booking online, redBus offers a lot of redDeals to book the bus ticket on budget.</li></ul> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> How does the transaction appear on my card / account statement? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <p>Transactions on redBus will appear as REDBUS.IN, <a href="http://www.redbus.in/" target="_self">www.redbus.in</a> in your bank statement.</p> </span> </div> </div> </div> <div class="faqQnaSection hide" style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 1.5rem; width: 100%;"> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> Can I cancel my bus ticket online? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <p>Yes you can cancel bus tickets online, Most of the tickets can be canceled online. However, there are some bus tickets that can only be canceled through our call center.However please note that the cancellation fee and cancellation period may differ for specific bus services. Please contact any of our executives for cancellation details on any specific service.</p> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> How can I cancel my bus ticket online? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <p>To cancel the bus ticket online, you need to click on the cancellation link provided on our home page. Enter your ticket number and the e-mail ID that was provided at the time of bus booking and click on cancel ticket.</p> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> I missed the bus. Do I get a refund? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <p>redBus provides a 100% refund if the bus is missed due to either redBus or its partner company's fault. However, if the bus is missed due to any other reason not directly related to redBus no refund is provided.</p> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> How can I get a refund in case I cancel my ticket? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <p>The refund is provided as per cancellation policy of the operator. The refund can be credited to the source of payment (Example: debit card, credit card, net banking) or credited to redBus wallet. Wallet credit can be used for bus booking in future (within 6 months of cancellation).</p> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> What happens if the bus does not leave on time or is canceled? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <p>If your bus does not leave on time or is canceled, in such situations, you will need to consult the counter of the respective bus operators. You can also call the redBus customer care to discuss the appropriate actions.</p> </span> </div> </div> <div class="faqQuestionSection" style=" border-radius: 1rem; border: 1px solid #F3F4F9; padding: 1.75rem 1.5rem; font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; color: #1D1D1D; cursor: pointer;" itemscope="" itemprop="mainEntity" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question"> <div style="display:flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; font-weight: 700;"> <span itemprop="name"> How can I reschedule my bus tickets? </span> <i class="plusMinus icon icon-plusv2" style="font-size: 18px;"></i> </div> <div class="faqAns hide" itemscope="" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer"> <span itemprop="text"> <ol><li>To reschedule your bus ticket on redBus, follow these steps: Visit <a href="https://www.redbus.in/reschedule" target="_self">https://www.redbus.in/reschedule </a></li><li>Search for your bus ticket by entering your ticket number and registered email ID.&nbsp;</li><li>Verify your online bus ticket details and select the date to reschedule your journey.&nbsp;</li><li>Select a bus operator, verify every detail, and make your payment if any difference in bus ticket prices needs to be cleared.</li></ol> </span> </div> </div> </div> <div class="faqQnaSection hide" style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 1.5rem; width: 100%;">
